## **ğŸ¬ Opening Setup**

*â€œThe Emporium smells of dust, candlewax, and profit.â€*

The shop appears empty.

**DM Tip:** Encourage players to *touch everything*. The faster they trigger the Lockdown, the funnier it is.

## **ğŸª The Mirror of Futures Passed**

*Central puzzle \+ moral tutorial.*

A floor-to-ceiling mirror between chandeliers shows delayed reflectionsâ€”each playerâ€™s reflection wears improved gear.  
 When **all** players look together, runes shimmer across the glass.

### **Puzzle Summary**

* **Goal:** Discover that unity (â€œacting togetherâ€) releases real loot.

* **Trap:** Acting alone spawns hostile reflections.

### **Mirror Trigger Table**

| Player Action | Mirror Reaction |
| ----- | ----- |
| One player grabs item | Reflection freezes and smiles; eyes glow red. |
| Two players grab different items | Cracks form; reflections whisper each otherâ€™s names backward. |
| All players mirror each other | Reflections nod; loot manifests. |
| Any attack/selfish act | Mirror fractures; reflections crawl out (combat). |

### **Puzzle Solution**

* All stand shoulder-to-shoulder.

* Each imitates their reflectionâ€™s stance or â€œitem.â€

* Mirror liquefies â†’ Items appear (Uncommon gear, tailored).

* \+1 **Descent Mark** (Unity through Greed).

* **Failure:** triggers **Mirror Doppelganger Fight** (below).

## **âš”ï¸ Encounter: Mirror Doppelgangers**

## **âš™ï¸ Mechanics Overview**

### **ğŸ”‹ Power Overwhelming (New Mechanic)**

When the partyâ€™s total **Essence Pool â‰¥ 50** and one or more PCs drop below 50 % HP,  
 they may burn **10 Essence** to trigger **Power Overwhelming**:

**Effect:** For 1 minute (10 rounds):

* Gain \+2 to all rolls.

* Deal \+1d4 radiant or chosen element per attack.

* After effect: each user takes 2d6 Force damage (burnout).

* The Codex records this moment: â€œAssets exceeded design capacity.â€

**DM Note:** This replaces traditional â€œlimit breaksâ€ and teaches resource mastery.

## **âš™ï¸ Core Mechanic â€” Shifting Reflections**

* **Every 3 rounds or 1 minute of real time**, mirrors shift: corridors bend, doors move.

* Arcana (DC 15\) can â€œanchorâ€ one corridor temporarily (3 rounds).

* If a player stares too long into any mirror (more than 1 round), they risk a psychic echo.

**Psychic Echo (B-Subsystem Effect):**  
 Wis save DC 13 or take 1d4 psychic, lose 1 turn hearing your own voice whisper â€œYouâ€™ve been here before.â€  
 Clearing Abyssal disables this hazard permanently.

---

## **ğŸ§© Puzzle Phase â€” Aligning the Core Mirrors**

At the center stands a circular room of six floor mirrors, each with runes corresponding to one Path (A, B, S, L, I, M).  
 To exit, players must align at least **two Path runes simultaneously** with light beams.

**Checks:**

| Skill | DC | Effect |
| ----- | ----- | ----- |
| Arcana | 14 | Realign a rune safely. |
| Insight | 13 | Predict which mirror will shift next. |
| Strength | 12 | Hold mirror steady for one rotation. |
| Failure | â€” | Mirror fractures â†’ spawns 1d2 Mirror Phantoms. |

## **ğŸ§  DM SIDEBAR â€” *Managing Dorm Growth at the Table***

* **Treat upgrades as rewards, not chores.** Each new room \= new play loop.

* **Avoid choice paralysis:** offer 1â€“2 active upgrade options per act.

* **Keep travel fast:** Dorm visits should feel like progress, not downtime.

* **Let NPCs explain systems:** Custodian Core, Spinebreaker attendant, or Grancelor message handle tutorial dialogue.

* **Use Essence scarcity to create tension.** Every upgrade is a moral decision between power and comfort.

## **âš™ï¸ Phase 1 â€” Room Mechanics: â€œThe Three Eyesâ€**

The Hub operates as a *rotating trinity*: every 3 rounds, control shifts between Legion, Syndicate, and Arcane subsystems.  
 Each subsystem changes **hazard type** and **enemy tactics.**

| Subsystem Active | Hazard | Player Counter | Duration |
| ----- | ----- | ----- | ----- |
| **Legion** | Auto-turrets emerge from floor. Each round, Dex save 13 or 1d8 piercing. | Strength 14 or Disable Device 15 to jam turret. | 3 rounds |
| **Syndicate** | Holographic duplicates of PCs appear. Act one round later. | Insight 14 or Persuasion 13 to confuse. | 3 rounds |
| **Arcane** | Antimagic pulse waves nullify 1 spell/round. | Arcana 15 or Con save 13 to resist. | 3 rounds |

Players can disable one subsystem permanently by sabotaging its node (see Phase 2).

## **ğŸ§© Phase 2 â€” Node Sabotage Challenge**

| Node | Approach | DC / Mechanics | Success / Failure |
| ----- | ----- | ----- | ----- |
| Legion (North) | Disable turrets manually. | Sleight of Hand 14 or Athletics 15\. | Disables turrets; gain \+1 Descent Mark. Fail â†’ spawn 2 Arcane Sentries. |
| Syndicate (East) | Jam illusion relay. | Insight 15 or Deception 14\. | Removes duplicates permanently. Fail â†’ gain \+1 Dark Debt (â€œrecorded infractionâ€). |
| Arcane (West) | Reroute power conduit. | Arcana 16 or Investigation 15\. | Antimagic field shuts down (magic usable). Fail â†’ 2d6 lightning surge. |

**Scaling:** Each failed attempt raises all DCs by \+1 (security tightening).

### **ğŸ§  Scene 6 â€” What It Means (for the DM)**

# **Appendix F â€” Gear Sets & Weapons (NEW)**

**Design Goals:** flavorful, fast, level-appropriate (Acts Iâ€“II), **2â€“3 piece sets** now, expandable later. Drop from Path mini-bosses/bosses; integrate with Range-Swarm loot logic. All items are **slot-based** (helm, chest, gloves, boots, cloak, ring, trinket, weapon) to allow set assembly.

## **F.0 Global Rules**

* **Set Bonus Tiers**: 2-piece minor, 3-piece signature.

* **Rarity**: Uncommon â†’ Rare within Book 1\.

* **Attunement**: Only the signature piece (usually chest/weapon) requires attunement.

* **Upgrade**: Feed Essence at Dorm Workshop (25 â†’ \+1 minor perk; 50 â†’ upgrade set bonus).

* **Scanner Tags**: Scanning a set piece hints at its missing siblings (â€œresonant rune gesture,â€ â€œcoin motif seam,â€ etc.).

---

## **F.1 Infernal Set â€” â€œClerk of the Twinflameâ€**

* **Slots**: Helm (Visor of Clause-Sight), Gloves (Ember Tally), Cloak (Ledger Ash)

* **Drops**: Q1 mini-boss (Helm), Q2 adjudicator (Gloves), Q3/Final (Cloak).

 Baelthorne, Auditor of the Dominion, assigns the party to clean up **Account \#666-73-D**, the *Twinflame Case*â€”two clerics whose shared miracle collapsed the books.

**Play feel:** dark bureaucracy meets heist-fantasy.

### **ğŸ§  DESIGN LOGIC**

Each Path not only represents a **narrative faction**, but also a **functional subsystem** of the Emporium:

* **Syndicate:** Logistics & planning layer (mission selection, resource prediction).

* **Arcane:** Infrastructure & system hacking (puzzle / traps / wards).

* **Infernal:** Social & negotiation layer (contracts, diplomacy, loopholes).

* **Iron Legion:** Security & enforcement (combat layer, field control).

* **Abyssal:** Containment & retrieval (treasure, breach, or stealth missions).

* **Monstrous:** Sanitation & repair (body-horror support, mutation fixes).

Together, they form a **six-role raid party**:

â€œOne builds the plan.  
 One opens the door.  
 One talks through the guards.  
 One breaks the wall.  
 One cleans the mess.  
 One steals the light.â€

---

* **Dormitory Upgrade Slots:** Each Path adds a new â€œroomâ€ or system.

  * Arcane â†’ Console Distillery

  * Infernal â†’ Contract Burner

  * Iron â†’ Foundry Bay

  * Abyssal â†’ Containment Core

  * Syndicate â†’ Planning Table

  * Monstrous â†’ Vivarium / Bioforge

* **Set Gear Progression:** Each Path grants 3â€“4 pieces per Book.

  * Book I \= 3-piece â€œIntro Setâ€

  * Book II \= adds 2 new pieces â†’ â€œFull 5-piece Master Setâ€

  * Full Set Bonus \= grants hybrid power reflecting that crew roleâ€™s ultimate mastery.

* **Book II (Audit Heist)**:  
   The team reforms as an *elite crew* for the Grand Reconciliation Heistâ€”each Pathâ€™s strengths will literally be used as â€œheist phases.â€  
   Example: Arcane disables temporal alarms â†’ Abyssal extracts artifact â†’ Infernal negotiates exit clause.

# **ğŸ’¼ SYNDICATE DOMINION â€” OVERVIEW**

**Role Archetype:** The Mastermind / Face / Broker  
 **Function:** Manipulator, deal-maker, agenda shaper  
 **Style:** Noir-market intrigue, velvet corruption, crime-thriller comedy  
 **Visual Aesthetic:** Gold-black neon, obsidian marble floors, hanging coins that glow with trapped souls  
 **Theme:** Profit as divinity. Information as weapon. Every smile is collateral.

**Signature Mechanics**

* **Social Heist Phases** â€” Structured like combat but with Negotiation Rounds instead of turns.

* **Reputation Meter** â€” Success/failure affects how much the Emporium trusts the party.

* **Mark Tokens** â€” Currency of deceit. Earned by manipulating or exploiting others; spent to rewrite one roll or contract clause.

* **Syndicate Path Gear (3-piece set)**
